62687   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} destMode;       \textcolor{comment}{/* Destination journal mode */}
62688   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pgszSrc = 0;    \textcolor{comment}{/* Source page size */}
62689   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pgszDest = 0;   \textcolor{comment}{/* Destination page size */}
62690 
62691 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifdef SQLITE\_ENABLE\_API\_ARMOR}
62692   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( p==0 ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_ab7984139894fa4451fa6acdc5867c6e9}{SQLITE\_MISUSE\_BKPT};
62693 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
62694   \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_af5a0a035d6f2e625f7fa5339365e8970}{sqlite3\_mutex\_enter}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a6ad9342dfbfe7f65e4f4c9c74b4d082b}{pSrcDb}->\hyperlink{structsqlite3_a7bcdded0e06fa908fe1a6df19c3dda21}{mutex});
62695   \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_afa05d700ca373993fe6b0525b867feff}{sqlite3BtreeEnter}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc});
62696   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a4fe8f1d9456d5a379a3b1f6ffd50fbe0}{pDestDb} )\{
62697     \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_af5a0a035d6f2e625f7fa5339365e8970}{sqlite3\_mutex\_enter}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a4fe8f1d9456d5a379a3b1f6ffd50fbe0}{pDestDb}->\hyperlink{structsqlite3_a7bcdded0e06fa908fe1a6df19c3dda21}{mutex});
62698   \}
62699 
62700   rc = p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_ac6509c6fe4cbf7bde170597172f8a288}{rc};
62701   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( !isFatalError(rc) )\{
62702     \hyperlink{struct_pager}{Pager} * \textcolor{keyword}{const} pSrcPager = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aa0b1925984c0d8606d760b8fa27a4d7c}{sqlite3BtreePager}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc});     \textcolor{comment}{/* Source pager */}
62703     \hyperlink{struct_pager}{Pager} * \textcolor{keyword}{const} pDestPager = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aa0b1925984c0d8606d760b8fa27a4d7c}{sqlite3BtreePager}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest});   \textcolor{comment}{/* Dest pager */}
62704     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ii;                            \textcolor{comment}{/* Iterator variable */}
62705     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} nSrcPage = -1;                 \textcolor{comment}{/* Size of source db in pages */}
62706     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bCloseTrans = 0;               \textcolor{comment}{/* True if src db requires unlocking */}
62707 
62708     \textcolor{comment}{/* If the source pager is currently in a write-transaction, return}
62709 \textcolor{comment}{    ** SQLITE\_BUSY immediately.}
62710 \textcolor{comment}{    */}
62711     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a4fe8f1d9456d5a379a3b1f6ffd50fbe0}{pDestDb} && p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc}->\hyperlink{struct_btree_a2bc66d19c064bb25ff335241f8c621df}{pBt}->\hyperlink{struct_bt_shared_ab3bcd3a6018a915020d48ef2f008f9a2}{inTransaction}==
      \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a44233c5892ed8292d0e28a52cfacd8a2}{TRANS\_WRITE} )\{
62712       rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2404c3c65a25e31de96f71d709c6b7c1}{SQLITE\_BUSY};
62713     \}\textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\{
62714       rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK};
62715     \}
62716 
62717     \textcolor{comment}{/* Lock the destination database, if it is not locked already. */}
62718     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK}==rc && p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a6eb18cf037082296899340a3b2200425}{bDestLocked}==0
62719      && \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK}==(rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a52d6706df15c67c22aa7d0e290c16bf5}{sqlite3BtreeBeginTrans}(p->
      \hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}, 2)) 
62720     )\{
62721       p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a6eb18cf037082296899340a3b2200425}{bDestLocked} = 1;
62722       \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aa1124ad3e3ee4dada2aa96eebd4e9c9a}{sqlite3BtreeGetMeta}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}, \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a5bc36402043264c669edd74b67987c54}{BTREE\_SCHEMA\_VERSION}, &p->
      \hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aefa4865e79a3a7868ca8177fa42130b1}{iDestSchema});
62723     \}
62724 
62725     \textcolor{comment}{/* If there is no open read-transaction on the source database, open}
62726 \textcolor{comment}{    ** one now. If a transaction is opened here, then it will be closed}
62727 \textcolor{comment}{    ** before this function exits.}
62728 \textcolor{comment}{    */}
62729     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} && 0==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a042d03b5e23a171bdb511e326a06b663}{sqlite3BtreeIsInReadTrans}(p->
      \hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc}) )\{
62730       rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a52d6706df15c67c22aa7d0e290c16bf5}{sqlite3BtreeBeginTrans}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc}, 0);
62731       bCloseTrans = 1;
62732     \}
62733 
62734     \textcolor{comment}{/* Do not allow backup if the destination database is in WAL mode}
62735 \textcolor{comment}{    ** and the page sizes are different between source and destination */}
62736     pgszSrc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a91f9dbfdbf95d6d9b955d1c7648b9fc1}{sqlite3BtreeGetPageSize}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc});
62737     pgszDest = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a91f9dbfdbf95d6d9b955d1c7648b9fc1}{sqlite3BtreeGetPageSize}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest});
62738     destMode = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_af59e923de7a57868bb8f10ba2634a072}{sqlite3PagerGetJournalMode}(
      \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aa0b1925984c0d8606d760b8fa27a4d7c}{sqlite3BtreePager}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}));
62739     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK}==rc && destMode==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a22111f604d197040fdf2740d6563e23a}{PAGER\_JOURNALMODE\_WAL} && pgszSrc!=pgszDest
       )\{
62740       rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a1ee0a0db43018cda5ee64cf78abbd675}{SQLITE\_READONLY};
62741     \}
62742   
62743     \textcolor{comment}{/* Now that there is a read-lock on the source database, query the}
62744 \textcolor{comment}{    ** source pager for the number of pages in the database.}
62745 \textcolor{comment}{    */}
62746     nSrcPage = (int)\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_ad098765ff19e404329c836462c185d95}{sqlite3BtreeLastPage}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc});
62747     assert( nSrcPage>=0 );
62748     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(ii=0; (nPage<0 || ii<nPage) && p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a1f54c0b52e2d890531dd9d7c9b8961b0}{iNext}<=(\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aec0c653e8dd16e4639caf2f8ea54f55c}{Pgno})nSrcPage && !rc; ii++)\{
62749       \textcolor{keyword}{const} \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aec0c653e8dd16e4639caf2f8ea54f55c}{Pgno} iSrcPg = p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a1f54c0b52e2d890531dd9d7c9b8961b0}{iNext};                 \textcolor{comment}{/* Source page number */}
62750       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( iSrcPg!=\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aeb787f0e765b267007078818f7e289a1}{PENDING\_BYTE\_PAGE}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc}->\hyperlink{struct_btree_a2bc66d19c064bb25ff335241f8c621df}{pBt}) )\{
62751         DbPage *pSrcPg;                             \textcolor{comment}{/* Source page object */}
62752         rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a22a53daafd2bd778cda390312651f994}{sqlite3PagerAcquire}(pSrcPager, iSrcPg, &pSrcPg,
62753                                  \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aaf8aca61da5571b284b23c77de0b353c}{PAGER\_GET\_READONLY});
62754         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{
62755           rc = backupOnePage(p, iSrcPg, \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a9dd340e56fb4b7fad4df339595b8d8a2}{sqlite3PagerGetData}(pSrcPg), 0);
62756           \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aa9d040b7f24a8a5d99bf96863b52cd15}{sqlite3PagerUnref}(pSrcPg);
62757         \}
62758       \}
62759       p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a1f54c0b52e2d890531dd9d7c9b8961b0}{iNext}++;
62760     \}
62761     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{
62762       p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a40c352fa743b4e8ae8ca29ab5c947f5c}{nPagecount} = nSrcPage;
62763       p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_af36e03f9d5806ab7fa1530a3950cc014}{nRemaining} = nSrcPage+1-p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a1f54c0b52e2d890531dd9d7c9b8961b0}{iNext};
62764       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a1f54c0b52e2d890531dd9d7c9b8961b0}{iNext}>(\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aec0c653e8dd16e4639caf2f8ea54f55c}{Pgno})nSrcPage )\{
62765         rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_afd1d7cc5f2e803af5e944f548e28f141}{SQLITE\_DONE};
62766       \}\textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( !p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a46ccfc2d96bd0831d4610c6da0738ecc}{isAttached} )\{
62767         attachBackupObject(p);
62768       \}
62769     \}
62770   
62771     \textcolor{comment}{/* Update the schema version field in the destination database. This}
62772 \textcolor{comment}{    ** is to make sure that the schema-version really does change in}
62773 \textcolor{comment}{    ** the case where the source and destination databases have the}
62774 \textcolor{comment}{    ** same schema version.}
62775 \textcolor{comment}{    */}
62776     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_afd1d7cc5f2e803af5e944f548e28f141}{SQLITE\_DONE} )\{
62777       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( nSrcPage==0 )\{
62778         rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a08d2026f82b067753a698376c12c0324}{sqlite3BtreeNewDb}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest});
62779         nSrcPage = 1;
62780       \}
62781       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} || rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_afd1d7cc5f2e803af5e944f548e28f141}{SQLITE\_DONE} )\{
62782         rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a550ba529de456d619365377b5528641c}{sqlite3BtreeUpdateMeta}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest},1,p->
      \hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aefa4865e79a3a7868ca8177fa42130b1}{iDestSchema}+1);
62783       \}
62784       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{
62785         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a4fe8f1d9456d5a379a3b1f6ffd50fbe0}{pDestDb} )\{
62786           \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2fc0d7e9d7e688a2a81ea4775dd12e33}{sqlite3ResetAllSchemasOfConnection}(p->
      \hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a4fe8f1d9456d5a379a3b1f6ffd50fbe0}{pDestDb});
62787         \}
62788         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( destMode==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a22111f604d197040fdf2740d6563e23a}{PAGER\_JOURNALMODE\_WAL} )\{
62789           rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2db3061b5c557699a47415ca0342ba01}{sqlite3BtreeSetVersion}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}, 2);
62790         \}
62791       \}
62792       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{
62793         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} nDestTruncate;
62794         \textcolor{comment}{/* Set nDestTruncate to the final number of pages in the destination}
62795 \textcolor{comment}{        ** database. The complication here is that the destination page}
62796 \textcolor{comment}{        ** size may be different to the source page size. }
62797 \textcolor{comment}{        **}
62798 \textcolor{comment}{        ** If the source page size is smaller than the destination page size, }
62799 \textcolor{comment}{        ** round up. In this case the call to sqlite3OsTruncate() below will}
62800 \textcolor{comment}{        ** fix the size of the file. However it is important to call}
62801 \textcolor{comment}{        ** sqlite3PagerTruncateImage() here so that any pages in the }
62802 \textcolor{comment}{        ** destination file that lie beyond the nDestTruncate page mark are}
62803 \textcolor{comment}{        ** journalled by PagerCommitPhaseOne() before they are destroyed}
62804 \textcolor{comment}{        ** by the file truncation.}
62805 \textcolor{comment}{        */}
62806         assert( pgszSrc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a91f9dbfdbf95d6d9b955d1c7648b9fc1}{sqlite3BtreeGetPageSize}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_aee09321030964a76af7f5e63ea20cb9c}{pSrc}) );
62807         assert( pgszDest==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a91f9dbfdbf95d6d9b955d1c7648b9fc1}{sqlite3BtreeGetPageSize}(p->
      \hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}) );
62808         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( pgszSrc<pgszDest )\{
62809           \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ratio = pgszDest/pgszSrc;
62810           nDestTruncate = (nSrcPage+ratio-1)/ratio;
62811           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( nDestTruncate==(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aeb787f0e765b267007078818f7e289a1}{PENDING\_BYTE\_PAGE}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}->
      \hyperlink{struct_btree_a2bc66d19c064bb25ff335241f8c621df}{pBt}) )\{
62812             nDestTruncate--;
62813           \}
62814         \}\textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\{
62815           nDestTruncate = nSrcPage * (pgszSrc/pgszDest);
62816         \}
62817         assert( nDestTruncate>0 );
62818 
62819         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( pgszSrc<pgszDest )\{
62820           \textcolor{comment}{/* If the source page-size is smaller than the destination page-size,}
62821 \textcolor{comment}{          ** two extra things may need to happen:}
62822 \textcolor{comment}{          **}
62823 \textcolor{comment}{          **   * The destination may need to be truncated, and}
62824 \textcolor{comment}{          **}
62825 \textcolor{comment}{          **   * Data stored on the pages immediately following the }
62826 \textcolor{comment}{          **     pending-byte page in the source database may need to be}
62827 \textcolor{comment}{          **     copied into the destination database.}
62828 \textcolor{comment}{          */}
62829           \textcolor{keyword}{const} \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2a0f0f4ae7001eb54351f77ea1cdbcfd}{i64} iSize = (\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2a0f0f4ae7001eb54351f77ea1cdbcfd}{i64})pgszSrc * (\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2a0f0f4ae7001eb54351f77ea1cdbcfd}{i64})nSrcPage;
62830           \hyperlink{structsqlite3__file}{sqlite3\_file} * \textcolor{keyword}{const} pFile = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a4994718ae281ffc714aa975c5b9b359d}{sqlite3PagerFile}(pDestPager);
62831           \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aec0c653e8dd16e4639caf2f8ea54f55c}{Pgno} iPg;
62832           \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} nDstPage;
62833           \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2a0f0f4ae7001eb54351f77ea1cdbcfd}{i64} iOff;
62834           \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2a0f0f4ae7001eb54351f77ea1cdbcfd}{i64} iEnd;
62835 
62836           assert( pFile );
62837           assert( nDestTruncate==0 
62838               || (\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2a0f0f4ae7001eb54351f77ea1cdbcfd}{i64})nDestTruncate*(\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2a0f0f4ae7001eb54351f77ea1cdbcfd}{i64})pgszDest >= iSize || (
62839                 nDestTruncate==(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aeb787f0e765b267007078818f7e289a1}{PENDING\_BYTE\_PAGE}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}->
      \hyperlink{struct_btree_a2bc66d19c064bb25ff335241f8c621df}{pBt})-1)
62840              && iSize>=\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a8cca202223a66c75a8bea6dabf8de43b}{PENDING\_BYTE} && iSize<=\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a8cca202223a66c75a8bea6dabf8de43b}{PENDING\_BYTE}+pgszDest
62841           ));
62842 
62843           \textcolor{comment}{/* This block ensures that all data required to recreate the original}
62844 \textcolor{comment}{          ** database has been stored in the journal for pDestPager and the}
62845 \textcolor{comment}{          ** journal synced to disk. So at this point we may safely modify}
62846 \textcolor{comment}{          ** the database file in any way, knowing that if a power failure}
62847 \textcolor{comment}{          ** occurs, the original database will be reconstructed from the }
62848 \textcolor{comment}{          ** journal file.  */}
62849           \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_ae82aaf561ce61faa15d4e228c45c3311}{sqlite3PagerPagecount}(pDestPager, &nDstPage);
62850           \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(iPg=nDestTruncate; rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} && iPg<=(\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aec0c653e8dd16e4639caf2f8ea54f55c}{Pgno})nDstPage; iPg++)\{
62851             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( iPg!=\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aeb787f0e765b267007078818f7e289a1}{PENDING\_BYTE\_PAGE}(p->\hyperlink{structsqlite3__backup_a845b397227de5c11118fa9db6b80ebde}{pDest}->\hyperlink{struct_btree_a2bc66d19c064bb25ff335241f8c621df}{pBt}) )\{
62852               DbPage *pPg;
62853               rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_ac690af087310cf9d64d04d8559be402e}{sqlite3PagerGet}(pDestPager, iPg, &pPg);
62854               \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{
62855                 rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_ad4b8aee028ee99575b0748b299e04ed0}{sqlite3PagerWrite}(pPg);
62856                 \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aa9d040b7f24a8a5d99bf96863b52cd15}{sqlite3PagerUnref}(pPg);
62857               \}
62858             \}
62859           \}
62860           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{
62861             rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a2baf986bff9120486e9acc5951494ea7}{sqlite3PagerCommitPhaseOne}(pDestPager, 0, 1);
62862           \}
62863 
62864           \textcolor{comment}{/* Write the extra pages and truncate the database file as required */}
62865           iEnd = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_adcd021ac91d43a62b2cdecf9a5b971a7}{MIN}(\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a8cca202223a66c75a8bea6dabf8de43b}{PENDING\_BYTE} + pgszDest, iSize);
62866           \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(
62867             iOff=\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a8cca202223a66c75a8bea6dabf8de43b}{PENDING\_BYTE}+pgszSrc; 
62868             rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} && iOff<iEnd; 
62869             iOff+=pgszSrc
62870           )\{
62871             \hyperlink{struct_pg_hdr}{PgHdr} *pSrcPg = 0;
62872             \textcolor{keyword}{const} \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aec0c653e8dd16e4639caf2f8ea54f55c}{Pgno} iSrcPg = (\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_aec0c653e8dd16e4639caf2f8ea54f55c}{Pgno})((iOff/pgszSrc)+1);
62873             rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_ac690af087310cf9d64d04d8559be402e}{sqlite3PagerGet}(pSrcPager, iSrcPg, &pSrcPg);
62874             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{
62875               \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a74a0f6424ae628af25f23f0a35f6ead3}{u8} *zData = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a9dd340e56fb4b7fad4df339595b8d8a2}{sqlite3PagerGetData}(pSrcPg);

62881             rc = backupTruncateFile(pFile, iSize);
62882           \}
62883

62885           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( rc==\hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a650d09c7bec7ddadb7c8aa3519dc842c}{SQLITE\_OK} )\{

62891         \}
62892

62896         )\{

62898         \}
62899       \}
62900     \}
62901   
62902     \textcolor{comment}{/* If bCloseTrans is true, then this function opened a read transaction}
62903 \textcolor{comment}{    ** on the source database. Close the read transaction here. There is}
62904 \textcolor{comment}{    ** no need to check the return values of the btree methods here, as}
62905 \textcolor{comment}{    ** "committing" a read-only transaction cannot fail.}

127895   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( zSql8 )\{

127897   \}\textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\{
127898     rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a9e34c7a5186dc9095e108e517eaac9f6}{SQLITE\_NOMEM};

127901   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_ae5a967ec6172298db98b6090bbd1dd9b}{sqlite3ApiExit}(0, rc);
127902 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

131445 \textcolor{comment}{    ** assert() was enabled at compile-time.  If X is true and assert()}
131446 \textcolor{comment}{    ** is enabled, then the return value is true.  If X is true and}
131447 \textcolor{comment}{    ** assert() is disabled, then the return value is zero.  If X is}
131448 \textcolor{comment}{    ** false and assert() is enabled, then the assertion fires and the}
131449 \textcolor{comment}{    ** process aborts.  If X is false and assert() is disabled, then the}
131450 \textcolor{comment}{    ** return value is zero.}
131451 \textcolor{comment}{    */}
131452     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a7d18cdd033a2fb27fe4d177fc734b1ae}{SQLITE\_TESTCTRL\_ASSERT}: \{
131453       \textcolor{keyword}{volatile} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x = 0;
131454       assert( (x = va\_arg(ap,\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}))!=0 );
131455       rc = x;
131456       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
131457     \}
131458

131460     \textcolor{comment}{/*}
131461 \textcolor{comment}{    **  sqlite3\_test\_control(SQLITE\_TESTCTRL\_ALWAYS, int X)}
131462 \textcolor{comment}{    **}
131463 \textcolor{comment}{    ** This action provides a run-time test to see how the ALWAYS and}
131464 \textcolor{comment}{    ** NEVER macros were defined at compile-time.}
131465 \textcolor{comment}{    **}
131466 \textcolor{comment}{    ** The return value is ALWAYS(X).  }
131467 \textcolor{comment}{    **}
131468 \textcolor{comment}{    ** The recommended test is X==2.  If the return value is 2, that means}
131469 \textcolor{comment}{    ** ALWAYS() and NEVER() are both no-op pass-through macros, which is the}
131470 \textcolor{comment}{    ** default setting.  If the return value is 1, then ALWAYS() is either}
131471 \textcolor{comment}{    ** hard-coded to true or else it asserts if its argument is false.}
131472 \textcolor{comment}{    ** The first behavior (hard-coded to true) is the case if}
131473 \textcolor{comment}{    ** SQLITE\_TESTCTRL\_ASSERT shows that assert() is disabled and the second}
131474 \textcolor{comment}{    ** behavior (assert if the argument to ALWAYS() is false) is the case if}
131475 \textcolor{comment}{    ** SQLITE\_TESTCTRL\_ASSERT shows that assert() is enabled.}
131476 \textcolor{comment}{    **}
131477 \textcolor{comment}{    ** The run-time test procedure might look something like this:}
131478 \textcolor{comment}{    **}
131479 \textcolor{comment}{    **    if( sqlite3\_test\_control(SQLITE\_TESTCTRL\_ALWAYS, 2)==2 )\{}
131480 \textcolor{comment}{    **      // ALWAYS() and NEVER() are no-op pass-through macros}
131481 \textcolor{comment}{    **    \}else if( sqlite3\_test\_control(SQLITE\_TESTCTRL\_ASSERT, 1) )\{}
131482 \textcolor{comment}{    **      // ALWAYS(x) asserts that x is true. NEVER(x) asserts x is false.}
131483 \textcolor{comment}{    **    \}else\{}
131484 \textcolor{comment}{    **      // ALWAYS(x) is a constant 1.  NEVER(x) is a constant 0.}
131485 \textcolor{comment}{    **    \}}
131486 \textcolor{comment}{    */}
131487     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a09256399837c34bafa294ccae9014fea}{SQLITE\_TESTCTRL\_ALWAYS}: \{
131488       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x = va\_arg(ap,\textcolor{keywordtype}{int});
131489       rc = \hyperlink{sqlite3_8c_a68d1f09d0baf7bc12a51d34a5c18fcfb}{ALWAYS}(x);
131490       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
131491     \}
